You will be seeing more of I Bike UNT in the future as we hope to grow our bike culture at UNT!</p><p> What will I Bike UNT be doing at EarthFest?<br /> - UNT PD will be engraving bicycles<br /> - Free On OnGuard Bulldog STD 8010 ULock for those that engrave their bike, while supplies last! <br /> - Safety Quick Checks for your bike<br /> - Bike Safety 101 class at 6:00 in Willis 136<br /> -
